### Probability Mass Function

![Graph with seats probability mass function not yet produced](average-seats-pmf-dielinkeguengl.png "Seats Probability Mass Function")

The following table shows the probability mass function per seat for the [poll average](average.html) for Die Linke (GUE/NGL).

| Number of Seats | Probability | Accumulated | Special Marks |
|:---------------:|:-----------:|:-----------:|:-------------:|
| 1 | 0% | 100% | Last Result |
| 2 | 0.1% | 100% |  |
| 3 | 13% | 99.9% |  |
| 4 | 58% | 87% | Median |
| 5 | 19% | 29% |  |
| 6 | 9% | 9% |  |
| 7 | 0.2% | 0.2% |  |
| 8 | 0% | 0% |  |
